      ⟨1v1⟩ ||◯ || Avighnam astu ||◯ || kiraṇa viyattiḥ candraghniḥ, dvijodaḥ ka:vi marutaraḥ, nahan· bhya [kta] pina [ka] śarira bhaṭāra,◯ mmilv aja:nma gave bhuvaṇa ◯ sira ta:ṣṭatanu (n) ṅaran [i] ra, sira ta:ṣṭadeśomidə [ṙ] pinakavəṅku, sira ta huripnikaṁ rat·, sira dumadyakən· vr̥ddhiniṁ janma ka
      ⟨1v2⟩beḥ, praṇapraṇī saṙvva hurip·, Ikanaṅ hurip· lavan avak·, śarira pamiṣanya ri sadha:radeṣa, gumavay ikaṁ saṙvva dadi, sira si§◯naṅguḥ purvvaniṁ janma ◯ Umijil taṅ a:ṣṭatanu rat·, nara mr̥gha paśu janma stavara, pakṣi śarīśr̥pa miṇa, prabhavaniṅ adharadeya ◯ prabhu ra:ma R̥ṣi tiga si§
      ⟨1v3⟩ra, prammaṇa rī rat·, pakənī bhuvaṇa, tuvī sira tan duḥka piśiki gurunī janma kabeḥ, linraranikiṁ candanira ṅkaṇa, sira tika śid (dha) ◯guru, sira haṣṭaga:ṇa gumavay īka vaṙtha sək lumraḥ ◯◯ Ikaṅ akṣaropamavak·, Ika ta guru ṅaranya, yeki ta vinastu hurip·, ya sinaṅguḥ guru
      ⟨1v4⟩laghu ◯ ya pinakamula canda, Avaknikaṁ guru laghu, lavan hurip masaṁyoga, Ummijil tikaṁ trigaṇa ◯ Adīnignikaṁ guru la:ghu, Aniga-ni⌈◯geṁ sagaṇa, yekaṣṭagaṇa ṅaranya, sama ha:byapare vaṙttha ◯ mvaṁ laku śloka nihan len· || || sakveḥ saṁ sujana:dihaṙṣa hirika [ṁ canda]
